< Text>
Pretty friendly peeps, but unfortunately they made errors in my order and the people in front and behind us.  The food was decent and the wait very long after ordering. I'm unsure why they close so early with 600 tents nearby....be nice (and prob very busy) if they stayed open til peeps came off the trail.  I honestly didn't give them a second chance this trip...perhaps another try next visit.  Chicken fritter sandwich was on very large ciabotta and pretty tastey.< /Text>

< Review>
If you go in here, there are two options for you specialty pizza and build your own. Well, I'm a small eater, so I chose build your own and picked small size. Small size came with 4 slices which was more than enough to fill my portion and then some. It was really delicious and what was even better was that the dining room was very spacy and cozy. They had some christmas decorations and lighting was just bright enough for good moody brightness.</Review>

< review>
Much has changed in the valley since I first visited decades ago, but one thing remains the same...Pizza Patio is still cranking out excellent pizza. Yes, there is often a long line, but it's worth the wait. The seating area has expanded over the years, so finding a shady table is no problem. Of course, you can take your food inside as well if you need to escape the weather.< /review>

I showed the pizza to a few people waiting in the line, and they all said it's raw. That is when they finally agreed to reheat it. <Rate>3<//Rate>< review>
The gym is fair  and it's not an amazing place. The customer service is OK. Their equipment is pretty old and they need to update it.
The personal trainers suck if you are enough sleep or you know how to work out and you want someone to just push you a little bit more. They are great for overweight people who have never worked out in their entire life. The personal trainers are average people were there to train you with the simple stuff.   The club makes a lot of money on the personal trainers. I bought a 12 session personal training.  I used three with one instructor who did not know his muscle groups. He thought doing military press was working the back muscles. Then I switched to a skinny girl who could barely lift 25 pound plates.    When I worked out with her and put more weights on she was shocked and impressed. She wasn't helping me much.    Again if you have never ever gone to the gym and may be helpful to take if you sessions with a personal trainer but I understand that they are basically making the club a lot of money and not helping you very much. <Date>1497998936922<//Date><username>Al Us</username><Resp>None< /Resp><pics>None</pics>< Review>
August 2016: Had a terrible experience with the kids tennis class' instructor Jana Acri. Not only her classes were extremely boring for a 5 year old kid (she had them take turns jumping on the floor ladder for half the class!), she was rude, and a borderline bully as an instructor. Her teaching instructions were not clear and when kids failed to follow her instructions, she kept saying that they need to pay attention, asserting various sorts of "punishments" on them, like sending them to the back of the line without taking a turn at whatever exercise they were doing.

My son told me that day that he hated tennis. Since we quit her class mid-session I've met several other parents who told me that they had a similar experience with that coach.

June 2017 UPDATE: : Raised my review from 1 to 5 stars to reflect updated experience. For the past 10 months my son has been taking tennis classes outside of Broadstone Racquet Club since the club only has 1 instructor that teaches 4-6 years old age range and we didn't want to go back to her. However, a few weeks ago we were able to put him into the next age range group (7-9 years old) class and that experience has been wonderful. His new coach Dennise Chauvet is really great. She has the perfect (for us!) balance of praise/discipline and techniques/games. Calm and professional, Dennise has her students' attention and respect. We are very happy with our tennis situation now and are grateful to another great coach at the club, Alejandro LaCruz, who was extremely helpful in finding a solution for our family so that we can all enjoy our tennis at the Broadstone Racquet Club.

Thanks to Dennise and Alejandro, we are now fans:)))<//Review>

My experience at Interstate Vape was incredible. Alex was very helpful and knowledgeable about their vaporizers and went the extra mile to make sure I was happy with my purchase.  They have a fantastic selection of vaporizers.  Everything from super quality high end to a affordable starter kits. They also have a great variety of juices.  The vibe there is awesome and everyone is extremely friendly.
